msg:This hotel is so nice! The staff are friendly and helpful. They accept foreigners, but at the current time you should make sure to bring a copy of a recent Covid test for check in. Super convenient if you're checking out the telescope. Just a few minutes drive away from the telescope center. There's a restaurant in the hotel, with a nice Chinese breakfast (noodles, wontons, fruit and veg), and they brought coffee out for us. There's also a nearby tourist village with a ton of hotpot places (most of which serve dog, so heads up on that). The rooms are lovely, shower was cool, and, at least at this time of year, there were very few other guests so it felt like we had the whole giant place to ourselves!

We were received by a young lady surnamed Xiao, who helped us solve many problems. Because I took my child to take the bus from Guiyang alone. When I left, I had to take the bus back to Guiyang from Pingtang Town. Tiantian Town is still far away from the Pingtang Town Bus Station. My lady helped us contact the long-distance shuttle bus. We were sent to the bus stop and gave us many small gifts before we left. My child and I were very embarrassed. Because during the few days we were there, Zhengzhou, Henan, was suffering from floods. The young lady cared and comforted me when she found out. She asked where we were, whether we were back home, and whether everything was normal at home. It's really caring and warm. My child said that the three of us must go to the Astronomy Town once to live in the Astronomy Guest House. I would like to express my gratitude to my little sister!
